    SELECT u.user_id, u.address, u.city_id, u.country_id, u.created_at, u.created_by, u.first_name, u.isdelete, u.last_name, u.modified_at, u.modified_by, u.phone, u.profile_image, u.role_id, u.state_id, u.status, u.userlogin_id, u.username, u.zipcode
    FROM users AS u
    WHERE NOT (u.isdelete)
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
INNER JOIN userlogin AS u0 ON t.userlogin_id = u0.userlogin_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r ON u0.role_id = r.role_id
